             Chicago's Ultimate Summer Patio Guide
            </h3>

            <div class="content simpleArticle site_article_box" id="site_article_box_1374">
             <p>
              <a class="link_as_text" href="/articles/2018/05/10/the-ultimate-patio-guide-to-summer-in-chicago">
               <img alt="Chicago" guide="" patio="" s="" src="http://assets.diningchicago.com/ckeditor/pictures/data/000/002/419/content/citymouse_anjalipinto_pressimage2_72417.jpg" style="margin: 0 5px 5px 0;" summer="" title="Chicago" ultimate="" width="150px;"/>

   	toggleRestaurants: function (map, visible) {
   		var markerImage = new google.maps.MarkerImage(document.location.protocol + "//" + document.location.host + '/images/icons/restaurant_location_small.png');
   		var markerManager = new MarkerManager(map, {trackMarkers : false, show: true});
   		var mapPoint;
   		var markerBounds = new google.maps.LatLngBounds();
   		if (visible) {
   			if (!map.markersList) {
   				map.markersList = [];
   			}
   			var markersList = map.markersList;
   
   			var length = GoogleMap.restaurants.length;
   			for (var i=0; i < length; i++) {
   				var rest = GoogleMap.restaurants[i];
   				mapPoint = new google.maps.LatLng(rest['lat'],rest['lng']);
   				markerBounds.extend(mapPoint);
   				var marker = new google.maps.Marker({
   					icon: markerImage,
   					position: mapPoint,
   					map: map,
   					visible: true
   				});
   				marker.setIcon(markerImage);
   				marker.target_location = rest['url'];
   				marker.r_name = rest['name'];
   				marker.address = rest['full_address'];
   				google.maps.event.addListener(marker, 'click', function(event) {
   					parent.document.location.href= this.target_location;
   				});
   
   				markersList.push(marker);
   				google.maps.event.addListener(marker, 'mouseover', function() {
   					this.setOptions({fillOpacity: 1});
   					var chTooltipHtml ='<div><strong>' + this.r_name + '</strong></br>' + this.address + '</div>';
   					tooltip.show(chTooltipHtml);
   				});
   				google.maps.event.addListener(marker, 'mouseout', function() {
   					this.setOptions({fillOpacity: 0.3});
   					tooltip.hide();
   				});
   			}
   		} else {
   			if (map.markersList) {
   				var length = map.markersList.length;
   				for (var i=0; i < length; i++) {
   					var marker = map.markersList[i];
   					marker.setMap(null);
   				};
   			}
   		}
   	}
   }
   
   $(document).ready(function() {
   	if ($.fn.fusionTableMap) {
   		var map_elem = $('.google_map');
   		map_elem.fusionTableMap({
   			fusion_document_id: '1dpQTOy3aqe9GOqdIprEG4BE-_L0WnGLw9jNbiPY',
   			fusion_column_names: ['name', 'geometry'],
   			map_center: [41.847685, -87.684827],
   			zoom_level: 13,
   			resize_to_fit: false,
   			fusion_selected_values: ["'Gold Coast'","'Magnificant Mile'","'Printers Row'","'Rush & Division'","'Streeterville'","'West Loop'","'Loop'","'South Loop'","'River North'","'West Town'","'East Village'","'Ukrainian Village'","'Bucktown'","'Lakeview'","'Lincoln Park'","'Old Town'","'Sheffield & DePaul'"],
   			scrollwheel: false,
   			streetViewControl: false,
   			zoomControlOptions: {
   			  style: google.maps.ZoomControlStyle.SMALL
   			},
   			panControl: false,
   			click_function: function(map, polygon) {
   				map.panTo(polygon.center_point);
   				map.fitBounds(polygon.bounds);
   				GoogleMap.toggleRestaurants(map, map.getZoom() > GoogleMap.markerTresholdZoom);
   			},
   			zoom_changed: function(map, newZoom) {
   				GoogleMap.toggleRestaurants(map, newZoom > GoogleMap.markerTresholdZoom);
   			}
   		});
   	}
